I bought tires at Costco and was told to get a four wheel wheel alignment done or my tire warranty would be void if I didn't.  My mechanic recommended Kim's tire and gave me their number. I called, scheduled an appointment for a convenient time. Arrived at Kim's tire on time was told it would be 45 minutes, got a call in 25 minutes that the alignment was completed. Price was very reasonable as it was less than I paid for a wheel alignment a couple of years ago when I bought tires at the place that sold me the tires. James was great, took time to explain that the car was way out of alignment and what was done to correct the problem. Immediately on driving away I noticed a huge difference in the way the car handled.  It handled so much better I was amazed! A bonus is that a few weeks later I noticed a 3 mpg improvement in trip computer. Five stars plus!<//review>

<Review>What an AWESOME find in Orange County! Was referred to this escape room by a friend. Can't thank her enough for introducing my friends and I to this wonderful, challenging, & fun escape room.

The room is located by the lab in Costa Mesa on Bristol & the 73 fwy. When you arrive in the business plaza, the entrance of the business is located in the back, in an upstairs unit. Little difficult to find so I hope these directions help.

Our group arrived a little bit earlier as recommended. We were greeted by the owner and gracious host Allen. He went above and beyond to make sure our group felt welcomed. He explained all the rules and really got us excited about the game. He even let us start our game a little later as my friends and I were enjoying an intense game of Cards Against Humanity he had in the waiting room Hahaha.

When we were done with the game (beat it with 30 seconds to spare), the owner took pictures and even recommended some other rooms for us to try in the area. Overall my friends and I has a wonderful experience and shared a great memory here. I'm definitely going to be an escape room addict now and cant wait to try this place again when they update the rooms and other escape rooms in Orange & LA county.

This store is the absolute best!if you have a chance, look at the attached pictures. Words do not begin to describe how large a selection of rums, whiskey, scotch, cognac, brandy, gin, etc. This store is slightly smaller than their main store off of El cajon boulevard.

Regardless of the type of alcoholic beverage you are looking for, they will have that selection.  The prices they charge for their selection are completely reasonable, too. They do have some drinks that they will have on sale. On the hole, everything in there is completely reasonable in price with a selection that isn't matched anywhere else in the San Diego area!<//Review>

< username>
J R< /username>
< text>
A one stop shop for fine spirits and craft beer. A hidden gem tucked away in sorrento valley. I knew the place existed, ive lived in the mira mesa area for a long time. but searching for different expressions of scotch to try led me here for the first time. To say their selection is amazing is an understatement.  Have you been wanting to try a particular whisky that you cant find anywhere locally? Do you have a favorite distillery but cant find their other expressions/offerings? Looking for vintage/rare? This place probably has it. Their prices are not too competitive, tbh, but i felt they were fair considering they stock so many different kinds that ive only ever seen online. If scotch isnt your thing, their bourbon and irish selection was just as impressive. Staff was super helpful and patient and made great recommendations. Will be visiting again when its time to try something new.</text>

<Rating>2< /Rating><name>A Wong<//name><Review>This store is selling sakes that are "EXPIRED and HAVE GONE BAD".  Please don't go into this store unless you want to walk out with bottles of expired alcohol.  I purchased three bottles of sparkling sake on 12/21/2012 from there and found out later that they were produced in 2009 and should be consumed within 120 days.  Plus, the sakes were not being stored properly.  They were just sitting on the self at room temperature when clearly on the bottle's label, "Keep Refrigerated"  No wonder not only there's no bubble when opened plus the taste was awful.  I even asked the owner about the expiration date because I saw a set of date (21.9.24) on the cap.  The owner assured that the sakes are fine and even if that's the expiration date, it should be either year of 2021/2024 so they are all good.  Later I googled and found out that the number 21 is era in Japan which corresponds to year of 2009 in Western era.  Even if the owner didn't know how to decode the date on the cap, he sure should have known those three bottles of sparkling sake have been on the shelf "FOREVER" and should be taken down instead of selling to people.  Since I bought the last three bottles I even asked if they will be getting more.  Answer I got was, yes, we always restock our inventory and in fact, order has been placed.  "LIAR! LIAR! LIAR!" Amazing, amazing (did I say... Amazing?) taquitos here. All food is vegan friendly. Tried their *warm* horchata this time too and it was also delicious. I've tried the tacos and the tamales here as well, both delicious. Their spicy sauce is SPICY. I usually ask for mild or a mix of mild and hot. Staff are all extremely friendly and if you order takeout and waiting around, they'll walk it up to you. Seating inside is tight and gets packed easily. <username>BernaDette Session< /username><rate>5< /rate>< Review>
Excellent food, affordable prices, ample portions, good vibes, friendly, knowledgeable staff. 100% vegan. Tasty authentic Mexican, vegan organic in addition to being so good! Food is as good as what you'd get eating in someone's home who is really good cook. We had tamales, of course, and their goodness rivaled that of my favorite Texas tamale offerings. The Taco plate was awesome as well. Used to be a food truck, & now they have a restaurant! Cool! One of my go to spots when visiting Cali's East Bay Area.
Tiny place, with more outside seating than in, which means takeout when the weather doesn't cooperate.
Enjoyed Flacos taquitos, black beans & rice at recent Vegan Soul Wellness Festival. And, yeah, they sold out before Festival ended, so missed out on banana leaf wrapped tamales, which Festival attendees raved about.<//Review>

<name>D Bennett<//name><Pics>None<//Pics><Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
Cozy atmosphere, friendly staff and delicious food. What more could you ask for. We came here because...well who could resist trying vegan Mexican food? We had the taquitos, tomales and huarache. I really don't have anything bad to say about any of it. The taquitos were crispy and flavorful and perfect for dipping in their fresh made salsa. The vegan ground in tomales was seasoned perfectly. I didn't eat the huarache but the person who did said it was a very delicious salad on top of thick fluffy corn tortillas. Everyone was very satisfied and would love to come back again.<//Review>
